    function recordOutboundLink(link, category, action) {

                ga('send', 'event', category, action);
            }



        if( ( action == 'link_site_agentie' || action == 'link_anunt_extern' ) &&
            typeof aTexte != "undefined" &&
            typeof aTexte.b_contact != "undefined" &&
            typeof aTexte.b_contact.sIdUnicOferta != "undefined" ){

            var id_lista = parseInt(get_params()['lista']);
            var iSursa = aTexte.b_contact.iSursa;
            if (typeof id_lista != 'undefined') {
                iSursa = iSursa + '|' + id_lista;
            }
            if( typeof aTexte.b_contact.sSursaText != 'undefined' ){
                iSursa = aTexte.b_contact.sSursaText;
            }

            $.post(aTexte.general.sPortalUrl + 'oferta/link-extern',
                    {'sIdUnicOferta' : aTexte.b_contact.sIdUnicOferta, 'iCategorie' : aTexte.b_contact.iCategorie, 'iTipTranzactie' : aTexte.b_contact.iTipTranzactie, 'iSursa' : iSursa})
        }

        if( typeof( link.href ) != 'undefined' && link.href.length ) {
            if(action == 'salveaza_anunt_add'){
              setTimeout('window.open("' + link.href + '", "_self")', 100);
            } else {
              setTimeout('window.open("' + link.href + '"' + ((action == 'link_site_agentie') ? ', "_blank"' : '') + ')', 100);
            }
        } else {

              setTimeout('window.open("' + link + '", "_self")', 100);
            } else {
              setTimeout('window.open("' + link + '"' + ((action == 'link_site_agentie') ? ', "_blank"' : '') + ')', 100);
            }
        }
    }
    function ignoreAgencyActions(action) {
        var agency = 'showEnergy';
        if (get_cookie(agency) == null) {
            return false;
        }
        var actions = ['contact_chat', 'contact_email', 'contact_telefon', 'contact_mobil_confirmat', 'contact_mobil_sms'];
        if (actions.indexOf(action) == -1) {
            return false;
        }


        return true;
    }
    function recordActionClick(target, category, action, bNonInteraction) {
        var leadAction = false,
            salveazaAutomatAnuntFavorit = false;

        switch (action) {
            case 'contact_email':
            case 'contact_telefon':
            case 'contact_email_galerie':
                leadAction = true;
                break;
            case 'contact_chat':
                leadAction = true;
                salveazaAutomatAnuntFavorit = true;
                break;
        }




        if(typeof(ga) != 'undefined' && ga.create) {
            if (!ignoreAgencyActions(action)) {
                if (category == 'action_click_imoagent') {
                    if (typeof aTexte != "undefined" && typeof aTexte.general != "undefined" && aTexte.general.iLogamEventuriAnalytics == 1) {
                        ga('send', 'event', category, action, target, {nonInteraction: typeof bNonInteraction != 'undefined'});
                    }
                } else {
                    ga('send', 'event', category, action, target, {nonInteraction: typeof bNonInteraction != 'undefined'});
                }

                if (leadAction) {
                    recordMotorRecomandareLeads(target, category, {nonInteraction: typeof bNonInteraction != 'undefined'});

                    recordLeadAction(target, category, action);
                }
            }
        } else {
            if (leadAction) {
                recordLeadAction(target, category, action);
                trimiteLogGoogleAnalyticsBlocat(target, category, action);
            }
        }



        if (salveazaAutomatAnuntFavorit) {
            if (typeof ANUNTURI_SALVATE !== "undefined") {
                ANUNTURI_SALVATE.detaliiOfertaPreluareOfertaFavoritaScript();
            }
        }
    }

    function trimiteLogGoogleAnalyticsBlocat(target, category, action) {
        if (typeof aTexte !== "undefined" &&
            typeof aTexte.general !== "undefined" &&
            typeof  aTexte.general.sPortalUrl !== "undefined"
        ) {
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                dataType: "json",
                url: aTexte.general.sPortalUrl + 'logare-google-analytics-blocat',
                data: {target: target, category: category, action: action},
            });
        }
    }

    function recordLeadAction(target, category, action)
    {
        if (typeof Indicative !== "undefined") {
            Indicative.buildEvent(action, {"target": target, "category": category});
        }
    }

    function recordMotorRecomandareLeads(target, category, nonInteraction) {
        if (window.location.href.indexOf('exprec') != -1) {
            var url = new URL(window.location.href);
            var leadFrom = 'widget_' + url.searchParams.get("exprec") + '_lead';

            ga('send', 'event', category, leadFrom, target, nonInteraction);
        }
    }

    function recordMotorRecomandareLeadsDev(target, category) {

            var leadFrom = 'widget_' + url.searchParams.get("exprec") + '_lead';

            console.log(target + ' - ' + category + ' - ' + leadFrom);
        }
    }

                                                                                                        <li><a tabindex="-1" class="sortare " data-val="iNrCamere-asc" href="javascript:;">Camere (cresc.)</a></li>

<script type="text/javascript">


        var modalPromoExitPopup_exit1646 = null;

    Date.prototype.yyyymmdd = function() {

        var yyyy = this.getFullYear().toString();
        var mm = (this.getMonth()+1).toString(); // getMonth() is zero-based
        var dd  = this.getDate().toString();

        return yyyy + '-' + (mm[1]?mm:"0"+mm[0]) + '-' + (dd[1]?dd:"0"+dd[0]);
    };

    data = new Date();
    var DataYmd = data.yyyymmdd()


        var modalPromoExitPopup_exit125 = null;

    Date.prototype.yyyymmdd = function() {

        var yyyy = this.getFullYear().toString();
        var mm = (this.getMonth()+1).toString(); // getMonth() is zero-based
        var dd  = this.getDate().toString();

        return yyyy + '-' + (mm[1]?mm:"0"+mm[0]) + '-' + (dd[1]?dd:"0"+dd[0]);
    };

    data = new Date();
    var DataYmd = data.yyyymmdd()



    $(document).ready(function(){


            modalPromoExitPopup_exit1646 = new modalPromoExitPopupClass('exit1646');
            modalPromoExitPopup_exit1646.init();


            modalPromoExitPopup_exit125 = new modalPromoExitPopupClass('exit125');
            modalPromoExitPopup_exit125.init();


    });

    function modalPromoExitPopupClass(numeModal) {
        "use strict";
        //url

        this.cookieNameShowedTimes = 'show_times_modal_promo_'+numeModal;
        this.cookieNameShowedToday = 'modal_promo_'+numeModal+'_showed';
        this.cookieNameConditions = 'modal_promo_'+numeModal+'_conditions';
        this.cookieNameDejaFolosit = 'modal_promo_campanie';

        this.modal = $('#modal-promo-exit-popup');
        this.init = function() {

            if (!allowed_to_set_cookie_category('functionale')) {
                return;
            }
            if (aTexte.general.iDeviceDetected != 1) {
                return;
            }

            this.recordUserActions();
            this.setEvents();
        };

        this.setEvents = function () {
            // Exit intent trigger
            this.exitIntent(document, 'mouseout', function(evt) {
                if (evt.toElement == null && evt.relatedTarget == null ) {
                    var modal = eval('modalPromoExitPopup_' + numeModal);
                    modal.showModal();
                };
            });
        };

        this.exitIntent = function(obj, evt, fn) {
            if (obj.addEventListener) {
                obj.addEventListener(evt, fn, false);
            } else if (obj.attachEvent) {
                obj.attachEvent("on" + evt, fn);
            }
        }

        this.showModal = function () {
            if (aTexte.general.pagina != 'lista') {
                return;
            }
            var showedTimes = get_local_storage_cookie(this.cookieNameShowedTimes);
            if (!showedTimes) {
                showedTimes = 0;
            }

            if (showedTimes >= 5) {
                return;
            }
            if (get_local_storage_cookie(this.cookieNameShowedToday)) {
                return;
            }
            if (!get_local_storage_cookie(this.cookieNameConditions)) {
                return;
            }
            var bCookieNameDejaFolositExista = {};



            bCookieNameDejaFolositExista.exit1646 = true;
            if (numeModal == 'exit1646') {
                $('#titlu_temporar').html("Vrei un apartament deosebit, situat &icirc;ntr-o zon&#259; premium a Bucure&#351;tiului?");
                $('#descriere_temporar').html("Un complex reziden&#355;ial situat &icirc;ntre parcurile Herastr&#259;u, Bazilescu &#351;i Kiseleff, ofer&#259; un stil de via&#355;&#259; select &#351;i un cadru de lux prin fiecare detaliu.<br />Vezi oferta!");
                $('#link_temporar').attr("href", "https://www.imobiliare.ro/ansambluri-rezidentiale/bucuresti/luxuria-domenii-residence-1646");
                $('#modal-promo-exit-popup').removeClass();
                $('#modal-promo-exit-popup').addClass('modal fade modal-promo-exit-popup-exit1646');
            }



            bCookieNameDejaFolositExista.exit125 = true;
            if (numeModal == 'exit125') {
                $('#titlu_temporar').html("Cau&#355;i Apartament &icirc;n Nordul Bucure&#351;tiului?");
                $('#descriere_temporar').html("Apartamente &icirc;nconjurate de natur&#259;, situate &icirc;n zona B&#259;neasa din Bucure&#351;ti. Apartamente noi &#351;i finalizate de dou&#259;, trei sau patru camere.");
                $('#link_temporar').attr("href", "https://www.imobiliare.ro/ansambluri-rezidentiale/bucuresti/greenfield-residence-125");
                $('#modal-promo-exit-popup').removeClass();
                $('#modal-promo-exit-popup').addClass('modal fade modal-promo-exit-popup-exit125');
            }


            var modalDejaFolosit = '';
            if (get_local_storage_cookie(this.cookieNameDejaFolosit)) {
                modalDejaFolosit = get_local_storage_cookie(this.cookieNameDejaFolosit);
            }

            if (typeof(bCookieNameDejaFolositExista[numeModal]) !== 'undefined' &&
                modalDejaFolosit != '' &&
                typeof(bCookieNameDejaFolositExista[modalDejaFolosit]) !== 'undefined' &&
                modalDejaFolosit != numeModal
            ) {
                return;
            }
            set_local_storage_cookie(this.cookieNameDejaFolosit, numeModal, 183);
            this.modal.modal('show');

            set_local_storage_cookie(this.cookieNameShowedToday, 1, 1);
            set_local_storage_cookie(this.cookieNameShowedTimes, showedTimes + 1);
        };

        this.recordUserActions = function () {
            if (aTexte.general.pagina != 'detalii') {
                return;
            }

            var cond = get_local_storage_cookie(this.cookieNameConditions);
            if (cond) {
                return;
            }

            var nrCam = 0;
            if (typeof dataLayer[0].propertyNumberOfRooms != 'undefined') {
                nrCam = dataLayer[0].propertyNumberOfRooms;
            }
            var bAfisareValida = false;



            if (bAfisareValida) {
                set_local_storage_cookie(this.cookieNameConditions, 1, 1);
            }
        };
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var ImoTiming = new TimingFrontend();
    var urlType = '';
            urlType = 'lista';
                sNumeCategorieDedicatRTB = 'Vanzare-Apartamente-Bucuresti';

    ImoTiming.setHost('https://www.imobiliare.ro/');
    ImoTiming.mark('document_head_end',iDocumentHeadEnd);
    ImoTiming.mark('document_body_end',(new Date().getTime()-iDocumentStart));
    if(urlType!='') ImoTiming.mark('url_type',urlType);

    jQuery(window).on('load', function() {
        setTimeout(function() {
            ImoTiming.mark('on_load',(new Date().getTime()-iDocumentStart));
            //single page call ox lista
            if(typeof(OXbanners) !== 'undefined' && OXbanners !== null) {

                OXbanners.loadBanners();
                ImoTiming.mark('load_opxads',(new Date().getTime()-iDocumentStart));
            }
            ImoTiming.send();
            if(window.performance && window.performance.timing) {
                    var timing = window.performance.timing;
                    var ImoTimingNew = new TimingFrontend();
                    ImoTimingNew.setHost('https://www.imobiliare.ro/');
                    if(urlType!='') ImoTimingNew.mark('url_type',urlType);
                    ImoTimingNew.mark('dns',timing.domainLookupEnd - timing.domainLookupStart);
                    ImoTimingNew.mark('connect',timing.connectEnd - timing.connectStart);
                    ImoTimingNew.mark('ttfb',timing.responseStart - timing.connectEnd);
                    ImoTimingNew.mark('html',timing.responseEnd - timing.responseStart);
                    ImoTimingNew.mark('dominteractive',timing.domInteractive - timing.domLoading);
                    ImoTimingNew.mark('domcomplete',timing.domComplete - timing.domInteractive);
                    ImoTimingNew.mark('onload',timing.loadEventEnd - timing.loadEventStart);
                    ImoTimingNew.send();
            }

            //lazy load restul
            if(typeof AsynchronousLoad == 'object') {
                AsynchronousLoad.lazyLoadPortal();

                var oImg = document.createElement('img');
                oImg.src = "https://www.imobiliare.ro/browsercache";
                document.body.appendChild(oImg);
            }
        }, 0);

        if(typeof(RtbHouse) != 'undefined' && typeof aTexte != 'undefined' && typeof aTexte.general != 'undefined' && aTexte.general.iIframeRTBHouseActiv == 1) {
            RtbHouse.generateIframe('other');





            if(typeof(sNumeCategorieDedicatRTB) != 'undefined') {
                RtbHouse.generateIframe('category', {sNumeCategorie: sNumeCategorieDedicatRTB});
            }




        }
    });

</script>
